# J. K. Rowling - Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix Concept Map - Concept Map

Concept map generated from: J. K. Rowling - Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix

## Concepts

### Level 0 - Foundational

#### House Points

House points are a scoring system in Hogwarts used to reward or penalize students, contributing to a competitive house cup awarded at the end of the school year.

**Also known as:** Points system

**Tags:** Harry Potter, school system, discipline and reward, Harry Potter universe, competition, Hogwarts, student assessment, wizarding culture, student behavior, discipline system

**Related:** Hogwarts Houses, House Points Docking

---

#### Hogwarts Houses

The four student houses at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry are Gryffindor, Hufflepuff, Ravenclaw, and Slytherin, each representing a different set of values and traits.

**Also known as:** Houses, Gryffindor, Hufflepuff, Ravenclaw, Slytherin, Wizarding Houses

**Tags:** Harry Potter, school system, student groups, wizardry, education, organization, Hogwarts, School Structure, Harry Potter universe

**Related:** House Points, Slytherin, Hufflepuff, Gryffindor, Ravenclaw, Quidditch

---

#### House Points Docking

House points docking is a disciplinary action in Hogwarts where points are removed from a student's house total as punishment for rule-breaking or misconduct.

**Also known as:** Point deduction

**Tags:** Hogwarts, discipline, Harry Potter

**Related:** House Points

---

#### Jinx

A jinx is a category of magical spell in the Harry Potter world that causes minor, often amusing or inconvenient effects, which are more severe than magic charms but less harmful than hexes and curses.

**Also known as:** Spell (inconvenience), minor curse, Magic curse

**Tags:** magic, spell, Harry Potter, defensive spells, offensive magic, Spells, Defensive Magic, magic spells, dueling, magical training

**Related:** Hex, Harry Potter characters: Snape, James Potter, Sirius Black, Remus Lupin, Peter Pettigrew, Lily Evans, Slug-vomiting Charm, Impediment Jinx, Stink Pellets, Jinxes, Counter-jinxes

---

#### Hex

A hex is a type of magical spell in the Harry Potter universe typically used to cause minor harm or discomfort to the target, often considered more troublesome than a jinx but less severe than a curse.

**Also known as:** Spell (minor harm)

**Tags:** magic, spell, Harry Potter, Magic Spells, Wizarding Combat

**Related:** Jinx, Harry Potter characters: Snape, James Potter, Sirius Black, Remus Lupin, Peter Pettigrew, Lily Evans, Reductor Curse

#### Examination Timetable and Procedures

The schedule and set of rules governing the O.W.L.s, including exams taking place over two weeks with theory exams in the mornings, practicals in the afternoons, and the special case of the Astronomy practical held at night.

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, exams, education procedures

#### O.W.L.s (Ordinary Wizarding Levels)

The O.W.L.s are standardized magical exams taken by fifth-year students at Hogwarts, assessing theoretical knowledge and practical skills in various magical disciplines over two weeks.

#### Hagrid

Rubeus Hagrid is the Hogwarts gamekeeper and Care of Magical Creatures teacher, known for his close connection to magical creatures and protective nature. He brought Grawp back from the giants and seeks help to teach him English.

#### Grawp

Grawp is a sixteen-foot-tall giant introduced in the story who has been brought back and hidden in the Forbidden Forest by Hagrid. He exhibits primitive behavior, such as ripping up twenty-foot pine trees and calls Hermione 'Hermy'.

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, character, magical creatures, Harry Potter, literature, fantasy creature

**Prerequisites:** Decree for the Reasonable Restriction of Underage Sorcery, 1875

**Related:** Decree for the Reasonable Restriction of Underage Sorcery, 1875, Underage wizards and magic use

---

#### Ministry of Magic Security Protocol

Procedures for admitting visitors to the Ministry, including stating name and business, badge issuance, security search, and wand registration.

**Also known as:** Ministry visitor procedures

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, security, Ministry of Magic

**Prerequisites:** Ministry of Magic Visitor Badge

**Related:** Ministry of Magic Security Check, Wand registration at the Ministry

#### Emotional confrontation in Dumbledore’s office

A key scene where Harry expresses intense pain, anger, and frustration with Dumbledore, highlighting his emotional turmoil.

**Also known as:** Emotional confrontation

**Tags:** literature, emotional development, character interaction

**Prerequisites:** Destructive anger

**Related:** Human pain as strength, Silver instrument

#### Seeker

The Seeker is a Quidditch player specialized in catching the Snitch to earn their team 150 points and end the match.

**Tags:** sports, Quidditch, player roles, Harry Potter

**Prerequisites:** Quidditch Match Scoring

**Related:** Tornados

---

#### Christmas Morning

The morning of December 25th celebrated in the wizarding world as in the non-magical world, characterized by gift-giving and festive family interactions.

**Tags:** holidays, calendar events, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Holiday Gift-Giving Traditions

---

#### Possession by You-Know-Who

A state where the dark wizard controls another person’s actions and memories, often causing the possessed individual to have memory blanks and lack control over their behavior.

**Also known as:** Demonic possession (in magical context)

**Tags:** dark magic, magical abilities, Harry Potter universe

**Prerequisites:** Practical Defensive Magic and its Use Against the Dark Arts

**Related:** Vision (Harry’s magical experience)

---

#### Vision (Harry’s magical experience)

A magical or psychic experience where Harry perceives events remotely or precognitively, such as the attack on Mr. Weasley.

**Also known as:** premonitory vision

**Tags:** magic, psychic phenomena, wizarding abilities

**Prerequisites:** Harry Potter’s Scar

**Related:** Possession by You-Know-Who

---

#### Underage Sorcery Charges

Formal allegations brought against underage witches or wizards accused of performing magic in violation of the Decree for the Reasonable Restriction of Underage Sorcery.

#### Of Age

Being legally recognized as an adult, usually implying certain legal rights and responsibilities, regardless of continuing education status.

#### Dumbledore's Army

A student organization at Hogwarts formed to oppose the Ministry of Magic's interference, named by Hermione and led or supported by Dumbledore. It was secretly meeting to train members in Defense Against the Dark Arts.

**Also known as:** DA, D.A.

#### Detention

#### Dobby’s departure from the Malfoys

An exception to the normal magical binding of house-elves, where Dobby was freed from servitude when presented with clothing, allowing him to leave the Malfoy household.

**Tags:** magic system, house-elves, event

---

#### Flagrate

Flagrate is a spell used to inscribe fiery marks in midair, such as a fiery ‘X’ on a door, which can serve as a magical marker or signal.

**Tags:** Magic Spells, Wizardry, Magic

**Prerequisites:** Incantation, Wand movement

---

#### Legilimency

A magical skill that enables a witch or wizard to delve into another person's mind under certain conditions and interpret their thoughts and feelings accurately.

**Also known as:** Legilimency magic, Mind-reading (magical)

**Tags:** magic, mental magic, wizarding skills, Harry Potter universe, Harry Potter lore, mind-reading, mind magic, offense

**Prerequisites:** Mind (magical context), Eye Contact (in Legilimency)

**Related:** Legilimens, Occlumency

---

#### Goal Hoops

Three vertical ring-shaped goals at each end of a Quidditch pitch through which players score points by passing the Quaffle.

**Also known as:** Quidditch Goals

**Tags:** Quidditch, Sports, Equipment

**Prerequisites:** Quidditch Scoring, Keeper (Quidditch)

---

#### Golden Snitch

A small, golden ball with silver wings used in Quidditch; catching the Snitch ends the game and awards 150 points to the catcher's team.

**Also known as:** Snitch

**Tags:** Quidditch, Sports, Equipment, Magic Sports, Sports Equipment, Harry Potter

**Prerequisites:** Quidditch Scoring, Seeker (Quidditch)

---

**Tags:** literature, politics, Harry Potter

**Related:** Ministry of Magic

---

#### Patronus Charm

A defensive magical spell that conjures a protective guardian known as a Patronus, often used to repel Dementors and invoked as a shield in dangerous situations.

**Also known as:** Patronus, Expecto Patronum

**Tags:** magic, defense, charms, defensive spell, spell, protection

**Prerequisites:** Professor Lupin, Silver Vapour

**Related:** Dementor Attack

---

#### Dementor's Kiss

A dark magical act performed by Dementors that involves sucking the soul out of a person's mouth, leaving them soulless and incapacitated.

**Also known as:** The Kiss

**Tags:** dark magic, magical attack, Dementors

**Prerequisites:** Soul, Happiness (magical context)

#### Wand (magical tool)

**Related:** Jack Russell terrier

#### Ordinary Wizarding Levels examinations (O.W.Ls)

Standardized magical exams taken by Hogwarts students in their fifth year to assess their proficiency in various magical subjects.

**Also known as:** O.W.Ls

#### Confusing and Befuddlement Draughts

Potions designed to induce hot-headedness, recklessness, and confusion in the drinker, often using plants like scurvy-grass, lovage, and sneezewort.

**Also known as:** Confusing Draughts, Befuddlement Draughts

**Tags:** Harry Potter universe, potions, magical medicine

**Prerequisites:** Sneezewort, Lovage, Scurvy-grass

**Related:** Sneezewort, Lovage, Scurvy-grass

### Level 2 - Intermediate

#### Fiery Cross

A Fiery Cross is a magical, burning symbol left on a surface, such as a door, typically created by the Flagrate spell to mark or indicate something important or previously tried.

**Also known as:** Fiery ‘X’ Mark

**Tags:** Magic Symbols, Wizardry, Magic

**Prerequisites:** Flagrate

---

#### Third Year at Hogwarts

The third year of Hogwarts schooling, during which Harry encounters Dementors and learns about Sirius Black and rescues him.

**Also known as:** Hogwarts Year Three

**Tags:** Harry Potter lore, education timeline

**Prerequisites:** Second Year at Hogwarts

**Related:** Hogwarts, Sirius's Head in the Fire

An effort by Hagrid to instruct Grawp in English to facilitate communication and help him understand that others wish him well, despite skepticism about its success.

**Tags:** magical creature education, communication

**Prerequisites:** Grawp's Social Challenges

**Related:** Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures

**Prerequisites:** O.W.L. (Ordinary Wizarding Level)

A student-led organization at Hogwarts formed to learn practical defensive magic against dark creatures and spells, outside official curriculum oversight.

The use of magic by individuals below a certain age, regulated and restricted by magical authorities to prevent exposure and misuse.

Magical laws regulating the use and ownership of wands, historically linked to social unrest such as goblin riots.

A magical spell used to render a target unconscious or immobile, commonly used in combat practice.

### Level 3 - Advanced

#### Wizarding Careers

Professional paths available within the magical community, each with specific subject or skill requirements, such as Healing, Muggle Relations, or Curse-Breaking.

**Also known as:** Magical Careers, Wizarding Professions

**Prerequisites:** N.E.W.T. (Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test)

#### Asiatic Anti-Venoms

A category of potion ingredients studied at Hogwarts used to counteract poisons from Asiatic magical creatures.

**Prerequisites:** O.W.L.

#### Ministry of Magic Improper Use of Magic Office

**Prerequisites:** Underage Sorcery

**Related:** Disciplinary Hearing (Ministry of Magic)

---

#### Defence Against the Dark Arts O.W.L.

**Also known as:** D.A.D.A. O.W.L.

**Tags:** Harry Potter, Exams, Magic Subject, Defence Against the Dark Arts

**Prerequisites:** Wizarding Magic Wand, Theory vs Practice in Magic Education
